<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jas.html>jas</a> (1411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jas.html>jas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jassen.html>jassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jasje.html>jasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">coat</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">outer garment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Volendam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who hasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> born and raised in Volendam.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jas.html>jas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jassen.html>jassen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jasje.html>jasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> or knave, especially as a trump card.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">troefboer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">troefzot</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***jasmine.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jasmine.html>jasmine</a> (9680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:jasmin.html>jasmin</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">يَاسَمِين</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yāsamīn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">یاسمین</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yâsamin</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">یاسمن</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yâsaman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Persian" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pal">yʾsmn'</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="pal-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">yāsaman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jasmine.html>jasmine</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jasmines</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several plants, of the genus <i>Jasminum</i>, mostly native to Asia, having fragrant white or yellow flowers.</li>
<li>The perfume obtained from these plants.</li>
<li>Any of several unrelated plants having a similar perfume.</li>
<li>A yellow colour.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:jasmine.html>jasmine</a> colour: <span style="background-color:EADD41; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

***jay.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a> (2822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">jai</i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"<a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a>"; Modern French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">geai</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">jai</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gay, merry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, so named due to its plumage, from Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*gāhi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quick, impetuous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ganhuz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ganhwaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sudden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaai.html>gaai</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">gay</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jays</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any one of the numerous species of <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> belonging to several genera within the family Corvidae, including <i>Garrulus</i>, <i>Cyanocitta</i>, <i>Aphelocoma</i>, <i>Perisoreus</i>, <i>Cyanocorax</i>, <i>Gymnorhinus</i>, <i>Cyanolyca</i>, <i>Ptilostomus</i>, and <i>Calocitta</i>, allied to the <a href = vnd.unilang:crows.html>crows</a>, but <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a>, more graceful in form, often handsomely colored, usually having a crest, and often noisy.</li>
<li>Other <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> of similar appearance and behavior.</li>
<li>Any of various large papilionid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Graphium" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Graphium"><i>Graphium</i></a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dull or ignorant person. <span class="use-with-mention">It survives today in the term jaywalking.</span>
<ul><li><b>1900</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>Harry</a> B. Norris, <i>Burlington Bertie</i> (song)
<dl><dd>Burlington Bertie's the latest young <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></b><br />He rents a swell <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> somewhere Kensington way<br />He spends the good oof that his <a href = vnd.unilang:pater.html>pater</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> made<br />Along with the <a href = vnd.unilang:brandy.html>Brandy</a> and Soda Brigade.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Promiscuous woman; prostitute.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="ante">a.</abbr></i> <b>1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">Shakespeare, William</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cymbeline" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Cymbeline">Cymbeline</a></cite>, act 3, scene 4, lines 50–51:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></b> of Italy, / Whose mother <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> her painting, hath betray'd him:</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bird</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jenny_jay" class="extiw" title="w:Jenny jay"><a href = vnd.unilang:jenny.html>Jenny</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/jay_pie" class="extiw" title="w:jay pie"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a> pie</a>, k, kae <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; bluejay, <a href = vnd.unilang:whisky.html>whisky</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">ignorant person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See Thesaurus:ignoramus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">promiscuous woman</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> See Thesaurus:promiscuous woman or Thesaurus:prostitute</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Respelling of the letter <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jy</i> (which see), by analogy with the following letter <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kay.html>kay</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jays</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">The name of the Latin-script letter <span class="mention">J</span></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A marijuana cigarette; a joint.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caitlin_Moran" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Caitlin Moran">Caitlin Moran</a>, <i>The Times</i>, 23 Mar 2009:
<dl><dd>Although sympathetic, my main reaction <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> to think: “Some people can handle it, and some people can’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>,” and then smugly light up a big fat <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jay.html>jay</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jegen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jegens.html>jegens</a></i>, with unetymological <i>-s</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gegin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gagin</i>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">jegen</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jenever.html>jenever</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">genever</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">geniver</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">genievre</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">genièvre</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Vulgar Latin from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">juniperus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">juniper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jerrycan.html>jerrycan</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***jetski.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jetski.html>jetski</a> (54193)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jetski.html>jetski</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***jeuken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jeuken.html>jeuken</a> (19848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">joken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">juecken</i>, long-vowel variants of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jocken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jucken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:juk.html>jukken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jukjaną</i>. The long vowels developed before the single consonants in the 2nd and 3rd person singular forms, e.g. Old Dutch 3rd person singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*jukit</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">jucken</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">itch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeuken.html>jeuken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to itch</li></ol>

***jicht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jicht.html>jicht</a> (18224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:jicht.html>jicht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*jiht</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*giht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jihtiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jicht.html>jicht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jicht.html>jichten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gout, a metabolic disease which painfully inflames the <a href = vnd.unilang:joints.html>joints</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jicht.html>jicht</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pijnlijke.html>pijnlijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontsteking.html>ontsteking</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gevolg.html>gevolg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> gekristalliseerd uraat in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewricht.html>gewricht</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:flink.html>flink</a> last <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jicht.html>jicht</a></b>.</i> </li>

***jihadist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a> (116346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jihad</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ist</i>. Attested from the 1910s in the sense of "a mujahid".<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.ch/books?id=LZ1VAAAAYAAJamp;q=jihadistamp;dq=jihadistamp;hl=deamp;ei=CHXKTaC3NMnJsgaKj72pAwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=1amp;ved=0CC0Q6AEwAA">[1]</a>
The adjectival sense of "pertaining to the <a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a> movement" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from the 1960s.<a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.ch/books?id=eN4_AQAAIAAJamp;q=jihadistamp;dq=jihadistamp;hl=deamp;ei=XHXKTauaHobBswaNz_SMAwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=2amp;ved=0CDIQ6AEwAQ">[2]</a><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.ch/books?id=K-VxAAAAMAAJamp;q=jihadistamp;dq=jihadistamp;hl=deamp;ei=G3bKTaGTNtHLswaOndSUAwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=1amp;ved=0CCwQ6AEwADgK">[3]</a><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.ch/books?id=pQJyAAAAMAAJamp;q=jihadistamp;dq=jihadistamp;hl=deamp;ei=7HXKTefaDsbDswar9-WmAwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=5amp;ved=0CD4Q6AEwBA">[4]</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jihadists</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who participates in a jihad; a mujahid.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mujahid</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">jihadi</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">takfiri</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Pertaining to the Islamic fundamentalist doctrine of jihadism.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li>jihadstrijder, moslimstrijder
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>'Nederlandse <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jihadist.html>jihadist</a></b><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verraders.html>verraders</a>'. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Afgeleide_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleide.html>Afgeleide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>jihadistisch</li></ul>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>jihadisme, jihadiste</li></ul>
<p><br />
</p>
</body> 
***jij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> (33)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ji</i>, northern form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jīz</i>, a northwest Germanic variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">ji</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">jie</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ye</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">jimme</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ihr</i>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> jingle (16423)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***jinx.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a> (35982)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jynx</i> in the <span class="Latn" lang="en">transferred sense</span> “a charm or spell”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jinxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A hex; an evil spell.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">curse</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoodoo.html>hoodoo</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Indian sign</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">spell</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A person or thing supposed to bring bad luck.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">jinxes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jinxing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jinxed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cast a spell on.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To bring bad luck to.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cause something to happen by mentioning it, usually sarcastically.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, Susane Colasanti, <i>When It <a href = vnd.unilang:happens.html>Happens</a></i>, Penguin (→ISBN), chapter <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=knkQLyHG0UwCamp;pg=PT185amp;dq=%22jinx+it%22amp;hl=amp;cd=8amp;source=gbs_apiv=onepageamp;q=%22jinx%20it%22amp;f=false">46</a>:
<dl><dd>“So you'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> all be near New York!” <a href = vnd.unilang:maggie.html>Maggie</a> says. “We don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know for sure yet.” <a href = vnd.unilang:sara.html>Sara</a> stresses. “Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a></b> it.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sally.html>Sally</a> Heinrich, <i>Hungry <a href = vnd.unilang:ghosts.html>Ghosts</a></i>, Hachette UK (→ISBN)
<dl><dd>I've no idea if she guessed what I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> intending to do. I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>  know why I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so reluctant to talk about it, <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> to her. Maybe I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> afraid that verbalising my intentions would <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a></b> it in some way.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>jinx</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Used after the same response <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> by two people simultaneously.</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1991</b>,  “Flaming <a href = vnd.unilang:moe.html>Moe</a>'s”, in  <cite>The Simpsons</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.imdb.com/title/tt0701098/quotes/qt0397691">[1]</a></sup>, season 3, episode 10, written by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Cohen_(writer)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Cohen (writer)">Robert Cohen</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Bart: I'm <a href = vnd.unilang:telling.html>telling</a> Mom and Dad! / <a href = vnd.unilang:lisa.html>Lisa</a>: You're <a href = vnd.unilang:telling.html>telling</a> who? / Bart: Mom and Dad! / <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>Girls</a>: MOM AND DAD? <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jinx.html>Jinx</a></b>! / Janey Powell: Now you can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> talk, '<a href = vnd.unilang:til.html>til</a> somebody says your name!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***jive.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a> (64541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a> attested in African-American and rural American culture. Frequently used to imply lying, verbal deception or trickery. <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>Has</a> a possible historical antecedent in <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gyve</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">jives</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jiving</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jived</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To deceive; to be deceptive.
<dl><dd><i>Don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> try to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>! I know where you <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> last night!</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To dance.
<dl><dd><i>You can dance, you can <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></b>, having the time of your life; <a href = vnd.unilang:ooh.html>ooh</a>, see that girl, watch that scene, diggin' the dancing queen!</i> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ABBA" class="extiw" title="w:ABBA"><a href = vnd.unilang:abba.html>Abba</a></a>, "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dancing_Queen" class="extiw" title="w:Dancing Queen">Dancing Queen</a>")</dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">jives</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dance style popular in the 1940–50s.</li>
<li>Swing, a style of jazz music.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> associated with jazz musicians; hepcat patois or hipster jargon.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Nonsense; transparently deceptive talk.
<dl><dd><i>Don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></b>. I know where you <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> last night.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often  derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> African-American Vernacular English.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">jives</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jiving</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">jived</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">jibe</i></span></span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>"<a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>Jive</a>" and "jibe" have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> used interchangeably in the US to indicate the concept "to agree or accord." While one recent dictionary accepts this usage of "<a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a>," most sources consider it to be in error.</li></ul>
<ul><li>See also "<a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a> turkey" for a related expression.</li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:jive.html>jive</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:levendig.html>levendige</a> Amerikaanse stijldans <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> jazzmuziek of rock-'n-roll, <a href = vnd.unilang:rond.html>rond</a> 1940 <a href = vnd.unilang:ontwikkeld.html>ontwikkeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:jitterbug.html>jitterbug</a>", <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Amerikaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:soldaten.html>soldaten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meegebracht.html>meegebracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> Europa <a href = vnd.unilang:tijdens.html>tijdens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweede.html>Tweede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereldoorlog.html>Wereldoorlog</a></li></ol>
